</td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_8c63f3c</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnSetCompleteScript</b></td><td><code></code></td></tr><tr><td><b>dwUID</b></td><td><code>194</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>ptLink</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arCallbacks</b></td><td><table><tr><th colspan="100%">QuestCallback</th></tr><tr><td><b>dwFlags</b></td><td><code>2</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start(idActor, idActorDetector)

	Hydra.ActorEnable(idArcherSpawner);
	
	local ambushSkeletons = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("Camp_KeironsPyre_SkeletonAmbush");
	
	Hydra.Wait(1);
	for i, idSkeleton in ipairs(ambushSkeletons) do
		Hydra.QActorAnim(idSkeleton, "Summoned_Animating_Ground");
	
--		Hydra.WaitForQEmpty(idSkeleton);
		Hydra.Wait(1)
	
		Hydra.ActorSetInvulnerable(idSkeleton, false);
		Hydra.ActorEnableAI(idSkeleton, true);
		Hydra.ActorSetTargetable(idSkeleton, true);
	
		Hydra.ActorClearAnimSetOverride(idSkeleton);
		Hydra.Wait(1);
